=================================INTRODUCTION==================================

I may not have every single item, but people have kindly provided me what
descriptions and such were missing. The main part of this guide is now complete
and I will be adding extras to help.  

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This stuff will be stuck into a new 'Special' section and integrated into the
original guide too, for your convenience.

Here's what I'm working on:
Oh, and you're welcome to help me with what I'm missing here. ^^

-What equips already come with recruits, and special ppl like Cid, Hurdy, etc.
 *(Status:Retired)*

-Which missions give out which loot
 *(Status:COMPLETE)*

Note: feel free to fill in the missing parts for me through email (:

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The main part of this guide is COMPLETE. =]

If anyone has questions, comments, or anything to contribute to the parts I've 
completed in this guide, feel free to email me at dragonkyrie@gmail.com. 
Notifying me about any errors or corrections in this guide is also welcome no 
matter how small, even if it’s just a typo. Oh, and please include the words 
'Final Fantasy Tactics A2' or something so I can tell what guide for what game 
you're talking about. Also, it makes sure that it's not spam. X3

*If it's been a very long time since the last revision of this guide, I may not
know the game as well anymore. Sorry!

===============================================================================
================================+GENERAL STUFF=================================
-----
-Items
-----
Items can either be equipment, loot, or items that can be used in battle.
Each has a different purpose.

<Equipment>
This is basically the things you can equip to your characters such as weapons,
armor, helms, and accessories. Many give different kinds of buffs and 
abilities for your characters. Most can be made and bought in the bazaar, but
there are several special items that can only be obtained by special means.

<Useable Items>
If your character has the 'Item' ability equipped, he or she can use items
during battle such as potions, ethers, echo herbs, etc. They can restore hp, 
restore mp, revive players, remove debuffs, or damage foes. Mirror Items is
a Seeq Ranger skill that makes items used by the seeq do the exact opposite
of its normal effect.

<Loot>
Loot is rewarded when you defeat a foe, usually by killing them. Loot is also
rewarded for completing a mission. Use the loot at the bazaar in the shop to 
unlock new equipment. You can also sell loot for more gil.

Oh, loot can also be stolen from monsters and enemies. However, I've noticed
that the loot dropped by enemies CHANGE. There is no solid setup. So if you're
in need of an item, it's best to do a mission that rewards that certain item
or use a move that reveals all of an enemy's loot, like Al-Cid's Interrogation.
Finding what you need should'nt be too hard, since enemies have a ton of loot.
One enemy has a total of 24 loots, 4 lv. 1 loots, 4 lv. 2 loots, 4 lv. 3 loots,
4 lv. 4 loots, 4 items, and 4 different amounts of Gil. It's the problem of
stealing the exact loot you need. Good luck. xD


*edit* Enemy loot in missions do NOT change, but enemies from the random
       monster encounters DO change.

If it's not a monster, they prabably also have armor, weapons, and accessories
that can also be stolen. I've noted that a few monsters have Ribbons and armor
but cannot be stolen. 

Uh...note that enemies can also steal from YOU. They can steal your items,
loot, gil, and even the armor you're wearing! You won't get it back. Once its
gone, it's gone. Your equipment, as well as the enemies' equipment, can also
be broken or destroyed, and again, you won't get it back. Gone. Forever. 

<What are 'Invisible' Items?>
Okay I kinda made this up but...yeah, the items actually do something so I 
thought they were worth mentioning.

Invisible items are things you apparently get from someone in a mission or
something, but doesn't show up as an usable item. Think of it as key items,
I guess. For example, Luck Sticks. Oh, and if the way how Illua banishes your
Judge all the time really annoys you, one of these items listed here will
really help. ;)

-Layouts
-----
<Equipment>
 _______________________
|(=-Name of Equipment-=)\
|------------------------*----->
|Description and any additional effects the item might have.
|
|Cost: Base price of item. 
|Bazaar: The section it is located in the bazaar and its grade.
|Ingredients: What loots are needed to make this item.
|
|If obtained only by a special means, I will put how to get it here.
| _______                  ___________               _________________       
|//Stats\\_______________ //Abilities\\____________ //Equippable Jobs\\______
|                        |                         |                         |
|Move:                   | What abilities this     | Jobs that can equip     |
|Jump:                   | item has.               | this item.              |
|Evasion:                |                         |                         |
|Speed:                  |                         |                         |
|Attack:                 |                         |                         |
|Defense:                |                         |                         |
|Magick:                 |                         |                         |
|Resistance:             |                         |                         |
|                        |                         |                         |
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`

<Useable Items>
 __________________
|(=-Name of Item-=)\
|-------------------*----->
|
|Description.
|
|Buy Price: How much it costs in the shop.
|Sell Price: How much it sells for.
|Effect: What the item does.
|Mirror Item: What the mirror effect is.
|
|Missions:
|-What missions rewards this item, the amount, and if the missions is 
| repeatable, meaning you can do it again and again when it shows up in the
| pub.
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`

<Loot>
 __________________
|(=-Name of Loot-=)\
|-------------------*----->
|
|Description.
|
|Sell Price: How much it sells for in the shop.
|Rank: The rarity of the item.
|
|Missions:
|-What missions rewards this item, the amount, and if the missions is 
| repeatable, meaning you can do it again and again when it shows up in the
| pub.
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`

<'Invisible' Items>

Name of Item
-----
Where: Where you get it.
Purpose: What you do with it.

|(=-Shining Lute-=)\
|-------------------*----->
|Element: Holy
|
|A lute made to accompany songs of devotion.
|
|Cost: 2000 Gil
|Bazaar: Hurdy's Request - A
|Ingredients: Flutegrass + Strawood
|
|Can only get two of these in the whole game. First can be made if you
|also get the Flutegrass after getting Strawood for Hurdy's instrument.
| 
|If missed, the only other way to get one is from the mission 'Rivalry of the
|Rupies'. To get this mission to appear, you must complete the mission 'Bangaa
|of the Rupies' or 'Nu Mou of the Rupies' to a total of I think 5 times. There 
|will then be a notice about buying the Rupies. Read it and then 'Rivalry of
|the Rupies' should be available. Note that once this mission is unlocked, you
|can no longer do the 'Bangaa or Nu Mou of the Rupies' missions. Complete the
|mission and you will receive the Shining Lute as your reward.

===============================================================================
================================+USEABLE ITEMS=================================
Listed in the order the game organizes the stuff. To use items, a character
must have the Item ability equipped.
 ____________
|(=-Potion-=)\
|-------------*----->
|
|A magick concoction that eases pain and heals wounds in the blink of an eye.
|
|Buy Price: 30 Gil
|Sell Price: 15 Gil
|Effect: Heals 30 HP
|Mirror Potion: Deal 30 damage to the target.
|
|Missions:
|-None
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`
 _______________
|(=-Hi-Potion-=)\
|----------------*----->
|
|A potion mixed for greater strength.
|
|Buy Price: 100 Gil
|Sell Price: 50 Gil
|Effect: Heals 100 HP
|Mirror Hi-Potion: Deal 100 damage to the target.
|
|Missions:
|-None
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`
 ______________
|(=-X-Potion-=)\
|---------------*----->
|
|The highest concentration potion available.
|
|Buy Price: 300 Gil
|Sell Price: 150 Gil
|Effect: Heals 200 HP
|Mirror X-Potion: Deal 200 damage to the target.
|
|Missions:
|-None
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`
 ___________
|(=-Ether-=)\
|------------*----->
|
|This tincture restores lost magickal power.
|
|Buy Price: 800 Gil
|Sell Price: 400 Gil
|Effect: Restores MP.
|Mirror Ether: Deplete 30 MP from the target.
|
|Missions:
|-Wanted: Barmaid! (3) (Repeatable)
|-Great Land Festival (4) (Repeatable)
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`
 ____________
|(=-Elixir-=)\
|-------------*----->
|
|This miraculous tincture completely restores both health and magickal power
|to the drinker.
|
|Buy Price: 1500 Gil
|Sell Price: 750 Gil
|Effect: Restores all of HP and MP of one character.
|Mirror Elixir: Reduce the target's HP and MP to single digits.
|
|Missions:
|-Bonga Bugle - Bloodfire (1) (Must serve 8 or 9 customers correctly.)
|
`----------------------------------------------------------------------------`

|(=-Antidote-=)\
|---------------*----->
|

===============================================================================
=============================+SPECIAL==========================================
Special as in...special means to obtain items other than the bazaar! 

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

                               -Auctions

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
At a point in the game, you should be taught how to play auctions, so I won't
be bothering to teach you. You should pay attention if you want to win some
powerful items easily. Once you win all the auctions at a city for the first
time, you will become region winner and the prize won't be territory, but
ususally decent equipment and weapons.

I can't say that the list is 100% complete, so if you have seen a prize not
listed here, feel free to tell me. xD If you don't know what an item is, I
suggest you search for it in the main section of this guide. ;)

(GP) means Grand Prize. To get the Grand Prize, you must win all the auctions.
Nice? You get all the auction prizes AND the grand prize. =]

Oh, almost forgot. You see the gauges at the end of auctions? If you fill them
up, you can get nice prizes, but only once. I'm only listing ones where you
get equipment, items, or money...

1st Place Gauge - Ribbon
2nd Place Gauge - Ether
3rd Place Gauge - 10,000 Gil

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

                               -Luck-sticks

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
What are luck-sticks? They are, in my terms, an 'invisible item'. Here's the
info if you're too lazy to look in the Invisible Item section:

Luck-Sticks
-----
Where: Bought for 1,000 Gil during Blackfrost at Fluorgis.
Purpose: Redeem it during Goldsun in Fluorgis to win an item.

Oh, and just to note, if you buy one, but don't redeem it, you won't be able
to use it. Yes, it expires after Goldsun. Congrats, you've just wasted 1,000
Gil. =] Even more, the Nu Mou who sells the luck-sticks will break your old
one.

Anyways, here's what you can win:

       Rank A: Brilliant Theorbo
       Rank B: High Arcana
       Rank C: Grimoire Stone
       Rank D: Darklord Crystal
       Rank E: Lightwing Crystal

          1st: Hurdy-gurdy
          2nd: Dark Matter
          3rd: Elixir
          4th: Zodiac Ore
          5th: Ether
          6th: Zincatite
          7th: Low Arcana
          8th: Gikhet Lead
          9th: Remedy
         10th: X-Potion
         11th: Hi-Potion
         12th: Gold Needle
         13th: Zinconium
         14th: Eye Drops
         15th: Potion

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

                               -Wayfarer Logs

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
You get one log for each quest listed below:

-The Forests of Loar
-The Lands of Loar
-The Towns of Loar
-The Seas of Ordalia
-The Wonders of Ordalia
-The Wonders of Loar
-The Forgotten Places

The mission known as 'Memories' will relieve you of the colored logs you get
from the listed missions, or should I say the Nu Mou will. You will get 
something in return though. You can do this again but don't forget to re-do
the listed missions to get the logs again.

No. of Logs:

1: X-Potion
2: Elixir
3: Mythril
4: Waterwyrd Crystal
5: ?
6: ?
7: Ribbon (First time only, consecutive times will earn you a Grimoire Stone.)

===============================================================================
=============================+'INVISIBLE' ITEMS================================

Judge Card
-----
Where: Cid gives it to you at some point, but Luso only mentions it after he
       finished the storyline battle in the mission 'Mountain Watch'.
Purpose: Summons Judge

Ewel's Card
-----
Where: The quest, "I've Been Had, Kupo!". 
Purpose: Prevents Illua or anything else from banishing your Judge. =] 
         Of course, if you break the law, he still goes bye-bye. 

Silverwhite(?) Magicite
-----
Where: After you finish the storyline mission, "Mountain Watch".
Purpose: I don't remember. o_O All I remember is that it's supposedly valuable
         and some guy yoinks it from you later on. x_X I -think- it's what's
         used to banish your Judge. 

Luck-Sticks
-----
Where: Bought for 1,000 Gil during Blackfrost at Fluorgis.
Purpose: Redeem it during Goldsun in Fluorgis to win an item. 

Ocktor Tome of Medicine
-----
Where: Obtained in the mission "The First Step".
Purpose: The client who gives it to you wants it back in the mission "The
         Last Step". He will give you the summon accessory for Zalera called
         Earrings of the Dead.
